<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:narcissus.html>narcissus</a> (45012)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:narcissus.html>narcissus</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">νάρκισσος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nárkissos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ultimately.html>ultimately</a> either <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pre-Greek_substrate" class="extiw" title="w:Pre-Greek substrate">Pre-Greek</a></span></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:related.html>related</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">νάρκη</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nárkē</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
